+#
+# Properties can have one of three forms:

+#

Modified: trunk/096/config/itemdesc.cfg
===================================================================
--- trunk/096/config/itemdesc.cfg	2005-10-27 18:11:35 UTC (rev 683)
+++ trunk/096/config/itemdesc.cfg	2005-10-27 18:48:28 UTC (rev 684)
@@ -1,65 +1,66 @@
-# //$Id$
+# $Id$
+#
+#
+#####################################
+#
+#  ITEMDESC.CFG - Item Definitions
+#
+#  Descriptors for Items, Containers, and Doors go here.
+#
+#  ITEM: The following may be specified for an Item:
+#  	Name			Name key (used only by GetObjtypeByName)
+#				- should be one word
+#	Color			starting color
+#	DecayTime		# of minutes before item decays (default is 10)
+#  	Desc			Description (see special rules)
+#  	Graphic			display graphic (defaults to objtype)
+#  	Invisible		if 1, this objtype is never seen.
+#	Lockable		is this item lockable
+#  	Movable			is this movable by default? default: use client files
+#  	RequiresAttention	block other actions until script detaches?
+#	Script			script to run on double-click
+#  	VendorBuysFor		base price vendors buy this for
+#  	VendorSellsFor		base price vendors sell this for
+#  	WalkOnScript		Script to start on walk-on
+#  	Weight			Weight, in stones
+#  	ControlScript		script to start on item creation, and on system load
+#	CreateScript		Script to start on item creation
+#	DestroyScript		run-to-completion script to run on destruction
+#  	SaveOnExit		1/0 - should the item be saved.
+#	DoubleclickRange	how close you have to be to use (default 1)
+#	Tooltip			tooltip text (maximum 256 characters)
+#	StrRequired		Strength required to equip this
+#	Newbie			Is this object type flagged 'newbie' by default
+#	BlocksCastingIfInHand	If this is in your hands, can you no longer cast?
+#	InsertNoise		sound to be played when item inserted into container
+#	RemoveNoise		sound to be played when item removed from container
+#
+#  CONTAINER: Everything that Item can have, plus:
+#  	Gump				Gump to display on container open
+#  	MinX			--\
+#  	MaxX			---  These define the legal bounds for items,
+#  	MinY			---  within the display gump.
+#  	MaxY			--/
+#	OnInsertNoise	sound to be played when items are inserted into the container
+#	OnRemoveNoise	sound to be played when items are removed from the container
+#
+#  DOOR: Everything that Item can have, plus:
+#	xmod		X modifier to door position to open/close
+#	ymod		Y modifier to door position to open/close
+#	doortype		wood/metal, used for determing sound.
+#
+#  Special rules for 'Desc' property:
+#	TODO: describe - same format as 'name' field in tiledata.mul
+#
+#  TODO: might be good to subdivide "user-definable" space so that shardops
+#	have their own space that "distribution" items won't clash with.
+#	same for packages, when that's done
+#
+#  TODO: Needs organized better.  Would be nice to be sorted by objtype,
+#	but that precludes grouping traps etc.
+#
+#####################################
 
-/////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
-//
-//  ITEMDESC.CFG - Item Definitions

+#
+#  Entries can contain the following properties:
+#      Name        Display name shown on login screen
+#      IP          IP Address of game server
+#                      Note: --ip-- uses your "Internet IP" address
+#                            --lan-- uses your "LAN IP" address
+#                            Otherwise, must be a numerical IP address.
+#      Port        Listening port of Gameserver
+#                      Note: This does not configure the server to actually
+#                            listen at that port - POL.CFG specifies that.
+#      IPMatch     IPAddr/Mask
+#                      If IPMatch lines are present for a server, that server
+#                      will only be displayed to clients connecting from IP
+#                      addresses matching those specified

+# $Id$
+#
+#
+###############################
+#
+# insertnoise.cfg v 0.1
+#
+# This config file contains information regarding sounds that are played
+#   specifically for insert/remove scripts.
+# This config file is used by insertsound.inc
+#
+# There are two fundamental sections to this file:
+#   Noises:  This section maps words to the noise address for the client to play
+#      By changing entries here, you will change what sound is played for all
+#      instances of that noise for all items that use it in the insert scripts.
+#   Special item entries:  This provides support for special items to have
+#      different sounds based on the amount of object inserted, such as gold.
+#      If there is no base (level 0 or 1) defined for the insert, then it will
+#      default to the itemdesc.cfg entry for that object.
+#
+# Important notes:
+#   - Special item entries are keyed by name
+#   - Changing a value for a sound will change all instances in insert scripts.
+#     Other references to sounds will not be effected, including constants defined
+#     elsewhere.
+#
+# Author: Valkyrie <Valkyrie at GatheringOrder.com>
+#
+###############################
 
 noises noisedefs
 {
@@ -35,7 +38,7 @@

+# $Id$
+#

+##############
+#
+# SpellID : same as the config key val- the ID of the spell
+# Name : the spells's name
+# SpellScript : the spell's SpellScript
+# Circle : the circle of the spell
+# Delivery : the mode of delivering the spell.
+#   direct : target something
+#   indirect : target an area
+#   notarget : no target necessary
+# Noto : casting a harmful spell on a blue will flag you criminal;
+#   casting a beneficial spell on a red will do the same.
+# PowerWords : the words of power for the spell
+# Animation : define a different spellcasting animation
+# animReps : caster will perform the spellcasting animation this many times,
+#   with 750ms passing in between. Overrides the default value in circles.cfg
+# extraWait : after finishing the animations, wait this many ms before spell
+#   actually goes off.  Overrides the default value in circles.cfg
+# Reagent : what regs the spell requires.
+#
+################
